We arrived in Weihai at exactly 3 pm, and we walked around but didn't have a meal. The next day, I arrived at Weigao Plaza and thought it would be the same. As a result, many restaurants in Weigao Plaza did not have closing time. This is the difference between the Economic Development Zone and the city center...
I suggest that friends who come to travel should stay in Weigao Plaza or the beach. You have to choose between business and scenery.
The hotel itself is very good!
